TABLE S5: Putative apicoplast targeted genes and expression profiles
Bozdech & Llinas et al.

This table contains all of the predicted apicoplast targeted ORFs from PlasmoDB.
The presence of each ORF on the DNA microarray is tabulated as well as whether
each ORF is present in the final analyzed set. Finally, the plastid ORFs in-phase
with plastid genome expression are listed.  Intensity ratios for all ORFs in the
analyzed set are also given.

Column 1: 551 Predicted apicoplast ORFs from PlasmoDB
Column 2: Predicted apicoplast ORFs found on the DNA microarray used
Column 3: Predicted apicoplast ORFs present in the final QC set
Column 4: Predicted apicoplast ORFs in-phase with plastid genome expression
Column 5: PlasmoDB Manual annotations for these ORFs

Microarray Intesity ratios BELOW!!!
Column 1: oligonucleotide ID				
Column 2: PlasmoDB ID				
Column 3: PlasmoDB Manual annotation				
Columns 4-49: Intensity ratios for all timepoints
